Notes:												
"1. EP4SGX110, EP4SGX180, EP4SGX230, EP4SGX290, and EP4SGX360 devices have two variants in the F1152 package optionone with no PMA-only transceiver channels (Transceiver Count of ordering code: F) and the other with eight PMA-only transceiver channels (Transceiver Count of ordering code: H)."												
2. Stratix IV GX devices without PMA transceiver channels do not have vertical migration to or from devices with PMA transceiver channels.												
"3. Altera's external memory interface IPs do not support placement of the BWSn pins outside the DQS/DQ group adjacent to the x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups where the write data pins reside. When using x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups that have 40 pins, BWSn inputs are not supported. "												
"However, if you are not using Altera's memory interface IPs and you are using x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups that have 40 pins, you can place the BWSn pins in a separate ×4 DQS/DQ group adjacent to the x32/x36 DQS/DQ group where the write data pins reside."												


"Pin Information for the Stratix® IV GX EP4SGX290 Device 
Version 1.6
"

Notes:												
"1. EP4SGX110, EP4SGX180, EP4SGX230, EP4SGX290, and EP4SGX360 devices have two variants in the F1152 package optionone with no PMA-only transceiver channels (Transceiver Count of ordering code: F) and the other with eight PMA-only transceiver channels (Transceiver Count of ordering code: H)."												
2. Stratix IV GX devices without PMA transceiver channels do not have vertical migration to or from devices with PMA transceiver channels.												
"3. Altera's external memory interface IPs do not support placement of the BWSn pins outside the DQS/DQ group adjacent to the x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups where the write data pins reside. When using x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups that have 40 pins, BWSn inputs are not supported. "												
"However, if you are not using Altera's memory interface IPs and you are using x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups that have 40 pins, you can place the BWSn pins in a separate ×4 DQS/DQ group adjacent to the x32/x36 DQS/DQ group where the write data pins reside."

Note:												
"1. Altera's external memory interface IPs do not support placement of the BWSn pins outside the DQS/DQ group adjacent to the x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups where the write data pins reside. When using x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups that have 40 pins, BWSn inputs are not supported. "												
"However, if you are not using Altera's memory interface IPs and you are using x32/x36 DQS/DQ groups that have 40 pins, you can place the BWSn pins in a separate ×4 DQS/DQ group adjacent to the x32/x36 DQS/DQ group where the write data pins reside."
